msg:The room is super good, very large, and very comfortable to stay in!
The hotel is located halfway up the mountain, with unobstructed views of the room balcony and the entire hotel, which is great! The hotel's hard and soft furnishings are very harmonious, with many plants planted, and there is also a rose street. When we went there, it was blooming.
The rice noodles for breakfast are delicious! There will be new breakfasts every day for two days of stay. The free afternoon tea is also good.
The private bath is hot spring water, and a milk bath is also given. The housekeeper will arrange for the lady to send the configured milk bath and a basket of petals to the room.
The front desk lady and the guys are very enthusiastic.
5 free travel photos are given, and the photographer is very nice! The photos are very beautiful!
It is also convenient to find the housekeeper to book other hot spring tickets and charter a car.

After staying in the hotel for one night, I laid the dirty sheets. The next day, I felt extremely itchy all over, and was bitten by some unknown insects. After consulting online, it was said that it was papular urticaria caused by insect bites. The people living together were also bitten, but not as serious as me. A woman who claimed to be the lobby manager of the hotel came to negotiate with me with a service staff. She looked through the sheets, but did not find the insects. She kept explaining that their sheets were changed for each guest. There were people living in this room before, but there was no such situation as mine. In the end, the hotel refunded the room fee for one night and paid the 200 yuan I consulted online. After refunding the room fee, the supervisor hoped that I would not give a bad review. I thought about forgetting it, but now, half a month has passed, and the bite is still swollen and red, and it itches and can't sleep. You need to take anti-allergic ***** and apply hormone creams every day. All of the above are my real experiences. I didn't expect that a hotel with 2,500 yuan could be bitten like this. I don't trust any hotel anymore.
